你能想象比被迫聆听无止境的絮叨更悲惨的命运吗？
She smiled and nodded as he wittered on，moving towards the door as the train drew into the platform.
Tā xiàozhe diǎnzhetóu tīng tā lāodāo，kàndào huǒchē xúxú shǐjìn yuètái，biàn mànmàn cháo mén zǒuqù。
她笑着点着头听他唠叨，看到火车徐徐驶进月台，便慢慢朝门走去。
I will never preach at you again.
Wǒ zài yě búhuì xiàng nǐ lāodāo le。
我再也不会向你唠叨了。
Her constant nagging ruffled her husband\'s feathers.
Tā zhàngfu bèi tā bùtíng de lāodāo shēng rěhuǒ le。
她丈夫被她不停的唠叨声惹火了。
I was turned off by her constant nagging.
Tā búduàn de lāodāoshēng shǐ wǒ gǎndào yànfán。
她不断的唠叨声使我感到厌烦。
She is always harping on the same old things.
Tā zǒngshì yí biàn yòu yí biàn lāodāo guòqù de shì。
她总是一遍又一遍唠叨过去的事。
She nagged to take a vacation.
Tā zǒng lāodāo shuō xūyào xiūjià。
她总唠叨说需要休假。
Her nagging went on endlessly.
Tā yìzhí lāodāo gè bùtíng。
她一直唠叨个不停。
譬喻
pìyù
metaphor
譬喻
《论语》：为政以德，譬如北辰，居其所而众星共之。
《Lúnyǔ》：Wéizhèngyǐdé，pìrú běichén，jūqísuǒ ér zhòngxīng gòngzhī。
In the Analects of Confucius, there are the following words: to run a country with morality wins a ruler the respect that the Pole Star gets, circled by numerous other stars.
譬如
pìrú
for example
譬如饮食习惯，南北各不相同。
Pìrú yǐnshíxíguàn，nánběi gèbùxiāngtóng.
Taking eating habits as an example, there are big differences between the north and the south.
譬如。

他说话喜欢打譬方，能把深奥的道理讲得生动通俗。
Tā shuōhuà xǐhuan dǎ pìfāng，néng bǎ shēnào de dàolǐ jiǎng de shēngdòng tōngsú。
He likes to make analogies when he speaks, which makes profound truth easy to understand.

老虎在角落里眼睛一眨不眨地看着他，不怀好意。

&quot;它难道不漂亮吗？&quot;我那7岁的小儿子眨着她的大眼睛问道。

in the twinkling of an eye

一眨眼的功夫他就把烧鸡给吃光了。

He ate up the entire roast chicken in a short time.

Tā yìzhǎyǎngōngfū jiù bújiàn le。
He disappeared in the blink of an eye.

支帐篷
zhī zhànɡpénɡ 
put up a tent
草地上有个半圆形的野营帐篷。

put up a tent
帐篷。
帐篷。

帐篷破了，不兜风

支架帐篷。

pitch a tent
搭帐篷
I was camping, suddenly a big brown bear came over my tent…I was petrified.
我正在露营，突然一只大灰熊走到了我的帐篷前……吓得我魂不附体。
I\'m more for buying him a new bike rather then a camping tent.
我更想给他买一辆新自行车，而不是野营帐篷。
I crawled into my tent to pack my things up.
我爬进帐篷去收拾我的东西。
Her home was a large tent with partitioned-off sleeping quarters.
她的房子是一顶大帐篷，里面有隔开的寝室。
Sleeping in a tent and having barbecue is real camping.
真正的野营就是睡帐篷和吃烧烤。
Diana\'s sleeping tent stood just next to the huge tree.
戴安娜睡觉的帐篷就搭在大树的旁边。
under canvas
在帐篷里
whose tent did you borrow?
你借了谁的帐篷？

昆廷用几根棍子支撑住帐篷。
Casey pounded the stake into the ground after he put up the tent.
凯西支好帐篷后，把木桩钉在地上。
Chuck helped me stake my tent.
查克帮我支了帐篷。
A little boy is standing at the threshold of their tent, pretending that he is a guard.
一个小男孩站在帐篷的门口，假装自己是守卫。
Felt can keep you warm in a cold tent.
在寒冷的帐篷里，毡子能让你暖和。
The felt tents protect the soldiers from the fierce climate here.
毡制帐篷可以帮士兵抵御这里恶劣的天气。
I was very grateful for the orange glow of the fire through the canvas tent.
Wǒ fēicháng gǎnjī fānbù zhàngpénglǐ tòuchū de júsè dēngguāng。
我非常感激帆布帐篷里透出的橘色灯光。
They decided to camp on the high table overlooking the valley.
Tāmen juédìng bǎ zhàngpeng zhāzài kě fǔkàn zhège shāngǔ de gāodì shàng。
他们决定把帐篷扎在可俯瞰这个山谷的高地上。
We slept in a tent during the camping trip.
Yěyíng lǚxíng qījiān，wǒmen shuì zài zhàngpéng lǐ。
野营旅行期间，我们睡在帐篷里。
They threaded their way round the ring towards the tent.
Tāmen chuānguò huánxíng dào zǒuxiàng zhàngpeng。
他们穿过环形道走向帐篷。
The tops were being set up for the circus show.
Rénmen zhèngzài dājiàn yòngyú mǎxì biǎoyǎn de dà zhàngpeng。
人们正在搭建用于马戏表演的大帐篷。
With the tent flap closed, the heat had been building up under the canvas.
Zhàngpeng shàng de ménlián fàngxià zhī hòu，rèliàng jiù kāishǐ zài fānbù xià jùjí。
帐篷上的门帘放下之后，热量就开始在帆布下聚集。
They owned a huge striped circus tent with its own seating.
Tāmen yōngyǒu yí gè dài zuòwèi de tiáowén mǎxì zhàngpeng。
他们拥有一个带座位的条纹马戏帐篷。
They compassed the city on horseback before returning to their camp.
Zài huídào tāmen de zhàngpeng qián，tāmen qímǎ ràozhe zhège chéngshì zǒule yì quān。
在回到他们的帐篷前，他们骑马绕着这个城市走了一圈。
An hour later they used the same tactics to gain entry to the other half of the camp.
Yí gè xiǎoshí hòu，tāmen shǐyòngle tóngyàng de cèlüè déyǐ jìnrù lìng yí bàn de zhàngpeng。
一个小时后，他们使用了同样的策略得以进入另一半的帐篷。
She had made no sound, from the minute of entering the tent until now.
Tā cóng jìnrù zhàngpeng dào xiànzài méiyǒu fāchū yìdiǎn shēngyīn。
她从进入帐篷到现在没有发出一点声音。
This guy regularly swung across the circus big top at a great height.
Zhège rén zài mǎxìtuán de zhàngpeng gāo dǐng shàng yǒu guīlǜ de dàngláidàngqù。
这个人在马戏团的帐篷高顶上有规律地荡来荡去。
He opened his eyes to find himself in a dimly-lit tent, seated upon hard muddy grass
Tā zhēngkāi yǎnjing，fāxiàn zìjǐ zài yí gè huī\'àn de zhàngpéng lǐ，zuòzài shī yìng de cǎodì shàng。
他睁开眼睛，发现自己在一个灰暗的帐篷里，坐在湿硬的草地上。
The rows of white tents are numbered to find them easily.
Wèi biànyú cházhǎo，yìpáipái de báisè zhàngpeng dōu biānle hàomǎ。
为便于查找，一排排的白色帐篷都编了号码。
The elders were gathered at the front of the tent.
Zhǎnglǎomen jùjí zài zhàngpeng de qiánmiàn。
长老们聚集在帐篷的前面。
On a windy day, guy ropes are needed to hold the tent upright.
Zài guāfēng de tiānqì lǐ，xūyào lāshéng lái bǎozhèng zhàngpeng bú huì bèi chuīdǎo。
在刮风的天气里，需要拉绳来保证帐篷不会被吹倒。
We brushed past trees and plants on the way to camp.
Wǒmen zǒuxiàng zhàngpeng shí，cāguò yìxiē shùmù zhíwù。
我们走向帐篷时，擦过一些树木植物。
A flimsy tent was chucked up without any trouble.
Yí gè bù jiēshi de zhàngpeng bèi cāngcù dājiàn qǐlái，méiyǒu fèi tài dà lìqi。
一个不结实的帐篷被仓促搭建起来，没有费太大力气。
The rest of the tent is then laid and pegged out.
Yúxià de zhàngpeng bèi pūhǎo dājiànle qǐlái。
余下的帐篷被铺好搭建了起来。
They rigged up a tent with old cardboard pieces.
Tāmen yòng jiù de hòu zhǐbǎn pīncòule yí gè zhàngpeng。
他们用旧的厚纸板拼凑了一个帐篷。
The children love to sleep out in tents, under the stars.
Háizǐmen xǐhuan zài hùwài xīngkōng xià de zhàngpéng lǐ shuìjiào。
孩子们喜欢在户外星空下的帐篷里睡觉。
The tents are spaced out by at least four metres.
Zhàngpeng zhījiān de jiānjù zhìshǎo sì mǐ。
帐篷之间的间距至少四米。
He threw up the tents in a hurry.
Tā cōngcōng dājiàn qǐ le yìdǐng zhàngpéng。
他匆匆搭建起了一顶帐篷。
No more refugees can be readily squeezed into tents.
Zhàngpéng lǐ bùnéng qīngyì jǐjìn gèngduō nànmín le。
帐篷里不能轻易挤进更多难民了。
We spread our sleeping bags on the dry floor of the tent.
Wǒmen bǎ wǒmen de shuìdài pū zài zhàngpeng zhōng de gānzào dìmiàn shàng。
我们把我们的睡袋铺在帐篷中的干燥地面上。
Level ground is best for parking and camp areas.
Píngdì zuì shìhé tíngchē zhā zhàngpeng le。
平地最适合停车扎帐篷了。
The living room was pure camp.
Qǐjūshì chúncuì jiùshì gè sùyíng zhàngpeng。
起居室纯粹就是个宿营帐篷。
He pitched his tent near the creek.
Tā bǎ tā de zhàngpeng dā zài nà tiáo xiǎoxī fùjìn。
他把他的帐篷搭在那条小溪附近。
The general\'s headquarters were a couple of large tents.
Nà wèi sīlìngguān de sīlìngbù jiùshì liǎngdǐng dà zhàngpeng。
那位司令官的司令部就是两顶大帐篷。
This tent sleeps six people.
Zhè dǐng zhàngpeng néng shuì liù gè rén。
这顶帐篷能睡六个人。
Winds buffeted the tent.
Kuángfēng bùtíng de chōudǎzhe zhàngpeng。
狂风不停地抽打着帐篷。
She fashioned a tent out of a sheet and a few sticks.
Tā yòng yíkuài bù hé jǐ gēn gùnzi dāqǐ yí gè zhàngpeng。
她用一块布和几根棍子搭起一个帐篷。
The circus tented near the town.
Mǎxìtuán de zhàngpeng dāzài zhège chéngzhèn fùjìn。
马戏团的帐篷搭在这个城镇附近。
After the hurricane destroyed our house, we had to improvise for weeks.
Fángwū bèi jùfēng cuīhuǐ zhīhòu，wǒmen zhǐnéng zài línshí zhàngpeng zhōng zhùshàng jǐ gè xīngqī。
房屋被飓风摧毁之后，我们只能在临时帐篷中住上几个星期。
The circus used a tent as their cookhouse.
Mǎxìtuán bǎ yí gè zhàngpeng yòngzuò tāmen de hùwài chúfáng。
马戏团把一个帐篷用作他们的户外厨房。
He was afraid of a fire in the circus tent.
Tā dānxīn mǎxìtuán de zhàngpéng lǐ huì fāshēng huǒzāi。
他担心马戏团的帐篷里会发生火灾。
They put up tents for the dining area.
Tāmen yòng zhàngpeng dā qǐle chīfàn de dìfang。
他们用帐篷搭起了吃饭的地方。
She looked haggardly out of her tent.
Tā dàizhe hěn qiáocuì de yàngzi zǒuchūle zhàngpeng。

Shuǐ de línjiè wēndù shì 100 shèshìdù——í zài biāozhǔn dī qìyā xià de fèidiǎn。
水的临界温度是100摄氏度——即在标准低气压下的沸点。

suffer repeated setbacks (or reverses)

几遭挫折
jǐ zāo cuòzhé
suffer repeated setbacks

遇到这么点挫折你就打蔫？

迭挫强敌
diécuò qiángdí 
inflict repeated reverses on a formidable enemy
我们应当把这次挫折引为鉴戒。
Wǒmen yīngdāngbǎ zhècì cuòzhé yǐn wéi jiànjiè。
We should take warning from this setback.
经受挫折
jīngshòu cuòzhé
go through setbacks
受到一点挫折用不着苦恼。
Shòudào yìdiǎn cuòzhé yòngbu zháo kǔnǎo。
You shouldn\'t get frustrated just because of a few setbacks.
力挫竞争对手
lìcuò jìnɡzhēnɡ duìshǒu 
beat the competition after tenacious effort
他多次遇到挫折，但从不气馁。
Tā duō cì yùdào cuòzhé，dàn cóngbú qìněi。
He never lost heart despite repeated setbacks.
他虽然遇到许多挫折，可是意志仍旧那样坚强。
Tā suīrán yùdào xǔduō cuòzhé，kěshì yìzhì réngjiù nàyàng jiānqiáng。
His determination remains as strong as ever despite all the setbacks he has encountered.
这场比赛咱们一定得赢，不能挫了锐气。
Zhèchǎng bǐsài zánmen yídìng děi yíng，bùnéng cuò le ruìqì。
We\'ve got to win the game, otherwise we\'ll lose our momentum.
几遭挫折
jǐ zāo cuòzhé
suffer repeated setbacks
受挫
shòucuò
be foiled; be baffled; be thwarted; suffer a setback
他近来工作上很不顺，比比受挫。
Tā jìnlái gōngzuò shàng hěnbúshùn，bǐbǐ shòucuò。
He is frustrated that his work has not gone very well recently.
挫折教育要成为孩子们的一门必修课。
Cuòzhé jiàoyù yào chéngwéi háizimen de yìmén bìxiūkè。
Frustration education should be arranged as a required course for all children.
最近遭遇三连败，球队的士气大受挫损。
Zuìjìn zāoyù sānliánbài，qiúduì de shìqì dàshòu cuòsǔn。
Recently, with three defeats in succession, the morale of the team has fallen greatly.
不受挫折教育，孩子永远长不大。
Búshòu cuòzhé jiàoyù，háizi yǒngyuǎn zhǎngbúdà。
Without being taught to accept defeat, children can never become mature.
遇到这么点挫折你就打蔫？
Yùdào zhème diǎn cuòzhé nǐ jiù dǎniān？
You will not be frustrated by the setback, will you?
为这点挫折，犯得上寻死吗？
Wèi zhè diǎn cuòzhé，fàn deshàng xúnsǐ ma?
Is it worthwhile committing suicide due to such a trivial setback?
他性格钢韧，从不怕挫折。
Tā xìnggé gāngrèn，cóngbú pà cuòzhé。
He has a strong, tenacious character, so he is never afraid of frustration.
因为找工作总是受挫，她整日郁郁寡欢的。
Yīnwéi zhǎo gōngzuò zǒngshì shòucuò，tā zhěngrì yùyùguǎhuān de。
She was unhappy all day long because she had difficulty finding a job.
他读起课文来，声音宏亮，语气抑扬顿挫。
Tā dúqǐ kèwén lái，shēngyīn hóngliàng，yǔqì yìyáng dùncuò。
He reads loud, and the tone is in cadence.
年轻人面对挫折不必惊怕，要学会镇定。
Niánqīngrén miànduì cuòzhé búbì jīngpà，yào xuéhuì zhèndìng。
Young people must learn to face challenges calmly.

Tā lǚzāo cuòzhé，dàn cóngbú qìněi。
He was thwarted time and again, but never became down-hearted.
在军事演习中，蓝军企图摸营，被红军挫败。

不经历些霜雪怎能知道如何面对挫折呢？

How can one know how to face setbacks if one hasn\'t gone through troubles?

Méiguīhuācóng lǐ zhǎngchū méiguīhuā。
玫瑰花丛里长出玫瑰花。
Museums around the country loaned the sculptures for the Rose Garden.
全国的博物馆都借出雕像给玫瑰花园使用。
He gave me rose flowers on my birthday.
我生日那天，他送了玫瑰花给我。

玫瑰花正在凋谢。
You should prune your roses in the spring.

你应该在春天修剪一下你的玫瑰花。
The roses need to be trimmed up.

那些玫瑰花需修剪。

Tā ài wén méiguī huāxiāng。

有些玫瑰花仍在盛开着。
Few roses were still blooming.
Shǎoshù méiguīhuā hái zài shèngkāi。
少数玫瑰花还在盛开。
She checks on her roses nightly.
Tā měi tiān yèjiān dōu jiǎnchá tā de méiguīhuā。
她每天夜间都检查她的玫瑰花。
The roses were transplanted from the garden to the florist

这些玫瑰从花园移植到花店里。
How cunningly the olive-green dress with its underskirt of rose-brocade fitted her perfect figure.
Gǎnlǎnlǜ de wàitào zài pèiyǐ méiguī tíhuā nèiyī，shì duōme shìhé tā wánměi de shēncái a。

The roses we planted finally blossomed out.
Wǒmen zhòng de méiguī zuìzhōng kāihuā le。
我们种的玫瑰最终开花了。

Yuándīng zhòngzhíle yì huātán de méiguī。
园丁种植了一花坛的玫瑰。
In Spring, my garden is always full of bees because of my roses.
春天时，我花园里的玫瑰总是引来满园的蜜蜂。
Root up the roses in the garden.
把花园里的玫瑰都连根拔了吧。

This place may be called Rose Garden.

这盒巧克力外面有一层玫瑰色的包装纸。

The box of chocolate is wrapped in rose paper.
这瓶香水是玫瑰香的，我很喜欢。

I like this bottle of rose-water very much.

这栋房子可以追溯到十八世纪晚期。
Making visual connections from space to space is a feature of the house.
Měi gé yídìng jùlí de shìjué liánjiē shì zhè dòng fángzi de fēnggé。
每隔一定距离的视觉连接是这栋房子的风格。
The builders were hammering away on the house.
Jiànzhù gōngrén zhèngzài qiāodǎ zhè dòng fángzi。
建筑工人正在敲打这栋房子。
This building has been in view for a long time, we don\'t know if they will actually build it.
Zhè dòng jiànzhù yǐjīng jìhuà hǎo hěn cháng shíjiān le，wǒmen bù zhīdào tāmen huìbúhuì zhēn de bǎ tā xiū qǐlái。
这栋建筑已经计划好很长时间了，我们不知道他们会不会真的把它修起来。
The vacant building is scheduled to be knocked down.
Zhè dòng kòngxián de dàlóu bèi ānpái chāichú。
这栋空闲的大楼被安排拆除。
They moved out of this building two weeks ago.
Tāmen liǎng zhōu qián bānlíle zhè dòng dàshà。
他们两周前搬离了这栋大厦。
The alleyway opened out into a space between four houses.
Xiǎoxiàng yánshēn dào sì dòng fángzi zhījiān de yípiàn dìfang。
小巷延伸到四栋房子之间的一片地方。
The building is partitioned into three sections.
Zhè dòng jiànzhù bèi fēnchéng sān gè bùfen。
这栋建筑被分成三个部分。
The headmaster\'s room is partitioned off at one end of the building.
Xiàozhǎng de fángjiān zài zhè dòng jiànzhù de yì biān，shì gékāi de。
校长的房间在这栋建筑的一边，是隔开的。
The building has been completely ploughed under.
Zhè dòng dàlóu yǐ wánquán bèi huǐ。
这栋大楼已完全被毁。
The old building was pulled down.
Zhè dòng jiù jiànzhù bèi chāidiào le。
这栋旧建筑被拆掉了。
The landlord was put in possession of the building.
Dìzhǔ yǐ zhīdàole nà dòng lóufáng。
地主已知道了那栋楼房。
I don\'t think this building is safe it was put up in only three weeks!
Wǒ rènwéi zhè dòng jiànzhù bù ānquán，tā jǐ gè xīngqī qián cái gāng jiànhǎo。
我认为这栋建筑不安全，它几个星期前才刚建好。
Fire raged through the building, leaving just a burnt outer shell.
Dàhuǒ sìnuèle zhè dòng dàshà，zhǐ liúxià shāojiāo de wàiké。
大火肆虐了这栋大厦，只留下烧焦的外壳。
A huge tower of smoke rose up behind the building.
Yì gǔ jùdà de nóngyān cóng zhè dòng jiànzhù bèihòu shēngqǐ。
一股巨大的浓烟从这栋建筑背后升起。
My parents were thinking about purchasing a new house.
Wǒ fùmǔ zài kǎolǜ mǎi yí dòng xīn fángzi。
我父母在考虑买一栋新房子。
My cousins and I live under the same rood.
Wǒ hé wǒ biǎoxiōngdìmen zhù zài tóng yí dòng fángzi lǐ。
我和我表兄弟们住在同一栋房子里。
The cost of buying a new house isn\'t chicken feed.
Mǎi yí dòng xīn fángzi de fèiyòng búshì xiǎo shùmù。
买一栋新房子的费用不是小数目。
The old wall goes back at least 10 meters under the current building.
Jiù qiáng zài zhè dòng jiànzhù xià xiàng hòu yánshēnle zuì shǎo shí mǐ。
旧墙在这栋建筑下向后延伸了最少10米。
There was a three-story building on the corner.
Guǎijiǎochù shì yí dòng sān céng gāo de lóufáng。
拐角处是一栋三层高的楼房。
The squatters had to surrender the building after the police moved in.
Jǐngchá cǎiqǔ xíngdòng zhīhòu，zhànlǐng zhèxiē fángzi de rén bùdébù jiāochū zhè dòng jiànzhùwù。
警察采取行动之后，占领这些房子的人不得不交出这栋建筑物。
They closed the deal on the building.
Tāmen jiéshùle yǒuguān nà dòng dàlóu de jiāoyì。
他们结束了有关那栋大楼的交易。
Several of the buildings were downright homely.
Zhèxiē jiànzhùwù zhōng yǒu jǐdòng shízàishì tài chǒulòu le。
这些建筑物中有几栋实在是太丑陋了。
This building is ugly, but architecturally interesting.
Zhè dòng lóu kànshàngqù hěn chǒu，dànshì cóng jiànzhùxué jiǎodù láikàn què fēicháng yǒuqùr。
这栋楼看上去很丑，但是从建筑学角度来看却非常有趣儿。
The wildfire scorched the forest and several homes.
Yěhuǒ shāohuǐle zhè piàn sēnlín hé jǐ dòng fángwū。
野火烧毁了这片森林和几栋房屋。

to monopoloize a conversation
(在谈话中)滔滔不绝，不给别人发言的机会；独占谈话
She will talk for hours on end.
她总是滔滔不绝地一讲就是几小时。

talk on and on in a flow of eloquence

The teacher was still holding forth after the bell had rung.
我对你的崇拜之情犹如滔滔江水延绵不绝。

My admiration for you is like the flowing water which never ends.

My admiration for you is like the unceasing flow of a river.
